One day, a man with red hair comes to backer street, and tell me his story.He is a really tall man with pure, eye-catching red hair. His hat is not in fashion anymore and his trench coat was definitely patched many times, with a weak smell of wine. There is a new scar on his jaw, which hasn't healed up yet. He shows a newspaper to me. It says that the boss of the Red-Headed League was about to pass away, and he wants to send his money to the people with purest red hair. He went to the interview and was chosen by the person in charge, who is a middle-aged man with a red hair. The other day, he was taken to a bar and Signed the document. But ever since then, that man with red hair disappeared and the money never appears. You signed up a document you couldn't understand!" Watson remarked. The lawyer said that it was a red-headed man, called Richard Brook, who claimed that he was of a high status in the Readed-headed league. [[R.Brook]]You noticed that his hand were covered by thick callus, and blackened by sun. Oops! When you shook hands with him, you could feel there is a piece of sands and soil in his hand. You kneaded it -- the same touch feeling as the sands in the River Thames. Meanwhile, there are calluses on his finger pulp. "Maybe he is not an upper class member?" You noticed that his fingers -- three of them was with expensive rings, and the forefinger has a white trace, meaning there was a ring before. You sunk into deep thoughts. You noticed dark red blood stains on a wine barrel; you observed and touched it, concluded that it may be here last night. And the dust covered on the top of this barrel was not as much as the other, it seemed to be rearranged. You concluded, "maybe a fight." You started to looked up at James, and fixing your eyes on his jaw. There was a bit of bruise on James's chin as if he was hit by a slap, and there were some scabs, which looked like caused by fingernails, near the slap trace. Watson asked. We all knew the woman is some sort of the center of the case. But the waiter replied, "no, of course." "Then Mr James, just think, think with your mind! Did you really not know her, or did you forget who she was because of being drunk?" Watson asked impatiently. "Just don't know!" "Hmm...Don't be fussy. Right leg...broken leg... I have an idea. I can find where is the woman coming from." You dashed to the front door, examining the footprints. You examined the footprint [[orderly]] or [[in a mess]].These neat footprints were left when people enter the pub. There were two special kinds of footprints: [[left prints remains more soil than right prints]] or [[right prints remains more soil than left prints]].
